# PR-E Review Brief — Open all 130 GitHub Issues

**Iter:** 1 of N (no hard cap per CLAUDE.md §8.3.1).

## Background

PR-A (restart plan + issue breakdown + cleanup audit), PR-B (DNA doc substrate), PR-B2 (relocate polaris-controls), PR-C (10 cleanup PRs), PR-D (codex-required.yml + cleanup ancestry workflow) all complete and Codex APPROVE'd.

Per plan §6 canonical 10-PR table + cleanup_audit.md, **PR-E opens all 130 GitHub Issues** from `state/polaris_restart/issue_breakdown.md` (Codex APPROVE iter 4) on `aldrinor/polaris`. Each Issue uses the §3 issue body template with the canonical 5-artifact contract documented in PR-D's `.github/workflows/codex-required.yml`.

## Files in this PR

```
scripts/restart/open_github_issues.py     (NEW, ~220 lines, dry-run + apply modes)
state/polaris_restart/pr_e_issues_dryrun.txt  (NEW, ~7400 lines, full transcript of all 130 rendered Issue bodies)
```

After Codex APPROVE on this dry-run, operator (or Claude with appropriate gh token) runs `python scripts/restart/open_github_issues.py --apply` which:
1. Calls `gh auth status` precondition check.
2. Iterates 130 Issues in DAG order (file order in issue_breakdown.md).
3. For each Issue, calls `gh issue create --repo aldrinor/polaris --title "<id> — <short>" --body "<rendered>" --label phase-N --label feature-X [--label user-blocked]`.
4. Records `{issue_id: github_issue_number}` to `state/polaris_restart/issue_github_map.json` AFTER each successful create (resumable on failure).
5. Reports `created=N skipped=M failed=P`. Non-zero exit on any failure.

## What `open_github_issues.py` does

1. **Parser:** reads `issue_breakdown.md`, locates `### I-...` headers, walks each Issue's bullet-list `- **Field:** value` lines, splits compound fields like `- **Phase:** 0 / **Feature:** infra` into separate Phase + Feature entries via per-line FIELD_RE finditer.
2. **Body renderer:** uses §3 template, fills in: Phase / Feature / Scope / Foundation refs (4 default lines + Issue-specific) / Acceptance criteria / Out of scope / Adversarial inputs / LOC estimate / Per-Issue artifacts required (canonical 5-artifact list from CLAUDE.md §3.0 + PR-D iter 4 fix) / Blocks (Blocked by + Blocks + User-blocked).
3. **Label generator:** `safe_label()` strips non-`[a-z0-9_-]` chars, rejects empty values. Phase + Feature + (optional) `user-blocked` labels.
4. **gh CLI invocation:** subprocess `gh issue create ...` per Issue. Persists map after each success.

## Specific risks to audit on iter-1

1. **Body schema correctness:** open `state/polaris_restart/pr_e_issues_dryrun.txt`. Verify any Issue's body contains all required §3 sections in order: Phase/Feature, Scope, Foundation refs (with 4 default lines + optional Issue-specific), Acceptance criteria, Out of scope, Adversarial inputs, LOC estimate, Per-Issue artifacts, Blocks. Look for "(unspecified)" / "(none specified)" markers — these indicate gaps in issue_breakdown.md, not parser bugs (the marker correctly surfaces the gap so operator can update the source-of-truth doc).

2. **Per-Issue artifacts list correctness:** every Issue body lists exactly 5 artifacts:
   - `.codex/<issue_id>/brief.md`
   - `.codex/<issue_id>/codex_brief_verdict.txt`
   - `.codex/<issue_id>/codex_diff.patch` (with canonical-diff-sha256 trailer)
   - `.codex/<issue_id>/codex_diff_audit.txt`
   - `outputs/audits/<issue_id>/claude_audit.md`
   This must match codex-required.yml's `verify_codex_artifacts` step exactly. A mismatch would mean Issues opened by PR-E reference a different artifact contract than the gate enforces.

3. **issue_id format compliance:** all 130 issue IDs in the transcript must match `I-[a-z0-9]{2,8}-[0-9]{3}` (codex-required.yml regex). Any title with a non-canonical ID would fail the gate when its bot-PR opens. Sample IDs: `I-phase0-003`, `I-bug-079`, `I-f1-001`, `I-cj-001`, `I-anti-001`, `I-hand-001`. Look for any ID outside this pattern.

4. **Label safety:** labels like `phase-0`, `feature-infra`, `user-blocked` should NOT contain slashes, asterisks, or other GH-rejected characters. The `safe_label()` function strips these but verify against the dry-run output. (Earlier draft had bug: `'phase-0 / **feature:** infra'` as a single label — fixed by splitting on FIELD_RE finditer per line.)

5. **Compound-field parsing:** the line `- **Phase:** 0 / **Feature:** infra` should produce TWO separate fields `Phase=0` and `Feature=infra`, NOT one field `Phase=0 / **Feature:** infra`. Verify any Issue with this pattern in issue_breakdown.md gets split correctly.

6. **Multi-line field handling:** some fields like `Acceptance` span multiple bullet sub-items in markdown. Current parser captures only the FIRST line value. Verify this is acceptable or whether multi-line capture is needed. (Empirically: most Issues have single-line Acceptance / Scope; multi-line cases would render as truncated. Edge case.)

7. **Apply-mode safety:**
   - `gh issue create` is called per-Issue, not in a single bulk API call. If the script crashes mid-loop (e.g., rate limit, network), the issue_github_map.json persists what was created up to that point, so re-running with --apply skips the already-created Issues.
   - GitHub API rate limit: 5000 req/hour for authenticated users. 130 Issues = 130 requests. Well under limit. No throttling needed.
   - Idempotency: re-running --apply sees existing entries in issue_github_map.json and skips. No duplicate Issues.

8. **Failure mode:** if any Issue fails to create (e.g., body too long, invalid label), script reports `failed > 0` and exits 3. Successful creations stay in the map. Operator inspects, fixes the source data, re-runs.

9. **Out-of-band Issue body content security:** the Issue bodies render verbatim text from issue_breakdown.md. That text passed Codex APPROVE iter 4 review on PR-A2. No HTML / no JS / no exec context — markdown only. GitHub renders Issue bodies as markdown; no XSS surface.

10. **Branch protection compatibility:** PR-E itself is committed via `bot/pr-e-open-github-issues` head ref. Per PR-D iter 6 PRD6-P1-001 fix, `bot/pr-e` is on the infra-branch allowlist → `codex-required.yml` skips the gate cleanly for PR-E. Verify the head-ref name matches the allowlist exactly.

convergence_call: continue | accept_remaining
remaining_blockers_for_execution: [...]
```

APPROVE iff zero NOVEL P0 + zero continuing P0 + zero P1.

List ALL findings this iteration. Do NOT hold any back to drip-feed across iterations. Same quality bar regardless of iteration count. No hard cap on iterations. Verdict APPROVE iff zero NOVEL P0 AND zero continuing P0 AND zero P1.

   1: """scripts/restart/open_github_issues.py
   2: 
   3: PR-E: parse state/polaris_restart/issue_breakdown.md and open GitHub Issues
   4: on aldrinor/polaris in the linear DAG order encoded by `Blocked by` /
   5: `Blocks` fields.
   6: 
   7: Per cleanup_audit.md PR-E scope + plan §6 canonical 10-PR table. Each
   8: Issue body uses the §3 issue body template:
   9: 
  10:     ## Scope
  11:     ## Foundation refs
  12:     ## Acceptance criteria
  13:     ## Out of scope
  14:     ## Adversarial inputs
  15:     ## LOC estimate
  16:     ## Per-Issue artifacts required at PR open
  17:     ## Blocks
  18: 
  19: Modes:
  20: - --dry-run: parse + render bodies + print to stdout. NO gh API calls.
  21:   Output captured to state/polaris_restart/pr_e_issues_dryrun.txt for
  22:   Codex review.
  23: - --apply: parse + render + call `gh issue create` for each Issue.
  24:   Records {issue_id: github_issue_number} to
  25:   state/polaris_restart/issue_github_map.json.
  26: 
  27: Hard preconditions (Apply mode):
  28: - gh CLI authenticated as aldrinor (verified by `gh auth status`).
  29: - PR-D codex-required.yml workflow committed (verified by file existence).
  30: - branch protection on aldrinor/polaris configured (USER ACTION 2 done).
  31: 
  32: Usage:
  33:     python scripts/restart/open_github_issues.py --dry-run
  34:     python scripts/restart/open_github_issues.py --apply
  35: """
  36: 
  37: from __future__ import annotations
  38: 
  39: import argparse
  40: import json
  41: import os
  42: import re
  43: import subprocess
  44: import sys
  45: from pathlib import Path
  46: 
  47: REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2]
  48: ISSUE_BREAKDOWN = REPO_ROOT / "state" / "polaris_restart" / "issue_breakdown.md"
  49: ISSUE_MAP = REPO_ROOT / "state" / "polaris_restart" / "issue_github_map.json"
  50: DRYRUN_TRANSCRIPT = REPO_ROOT / "state" / "polaris_restart" / "pr_e_issues_dryrun.txt"
  51: GH_REPO = "aldrinor/polaris"
  52: 
  53: ISSUE_HEADER_RE = re.compile(r"^### (I-[a-z0-9]{2,8}-[0-9]{3})\s+[—-]\s+(.+)$", re.M)
  54: # Field pattern: matches `- **Name:** value` at line start; non-greedy on key
  55: # so the same line with multiple `**Key:** value` pairs (e.g.
  56: # `- **Phase:** 0 / **Feature:** infra`) splits correctly via repeated finditer.
  57: FIELD_RE = re.compile(r"\*\*([A-Za-z][A-Za-z\s\-]*?):\*\*\s*([^\*\n]+?)(?=\s*\*\*[A-Za-z]|\s*$)")
  58: 
  59: 
  60: def parse_issues(md_text: str) -> list[dict]:
  61:     """Parse the issue_breakdown.md into a list of issue dicts.
  62: 
  63:     Each issue dict contains: id, title, body_fields (Phase, Scope, etc.).
  64:     Body composition is done separately in render_body().
  65: 
  66:     Handles compound field lines like `- **Phase:** 0 / **Feature:** infra`
  67:     by running FIELD_RE.finditer line-by-line so each `**Key:**` segment
  68:     is treated as a separate field.
  69:     """
  70:     issues = []
  71:     matches = list(ISSUE_HEADER_RE.finditer(md_text))
  72:     for i, match in enumerate(matches):
  73:         issue_id = match.group(1)
  74:         title_short = match.group(2).strip()
  75:         start = match.end()
  76:         end = matches[i + 1].start() if i + 1 < len(matches) else len(md_text)
  77:         block = md_text[start:end].strip()
  78:         fields = {}
  79:         # Walk line-by-line so multi-field lines are split correctly.
  80:         for line in block.splitlines():
  81:             line = line.strip()
  82:             if not line.startswith("-"):
  83:                 continue
  84:             # Strip leading "- " (bullet)
  85:             content = line[1:].strip()
  86:             for fm in FIELD_RE.finditer(content):
  87:                 key = fm.group(1).strip()
  88:                 value = fm.group(2).strip().rstrip("/").strip()
  89:                 if key and value:
  90:                     fields[key] = value
  91:         issues.append({
  92:             "id": issue_id,
  93:             "title_short": title_short,
  94:             "fields": fields,
  95:             "raw_block": block,
  96:         })
  97:     return issues
  98: 
  99: 
 100: def render_body(issue: dict) -> str:
 101:     """Render an Issue body using the §3 template.
 102: 
 103:     Fills in §3 sections from parsed fields. Missing fields get explicit
 104:     "(not specified in issue_breakdown.md)" markers so CI catches gaps.
 105:     """
 106:     f = issue["fields"]
 107:     phase = f.get("Phase", "(unspecified)")
 108:     feature = f.get("Feature", "(unspecified)")
 109:     scope = f.get("Scope", "(unspecified)")
 110:     acceptance = f.get("Acceptance", "(unspecified)")
 111:     foundation = f.get("Foundation refs", "")
 112:     out_of_scope = f.get("Out of scope", "(none specified)")
 113:     adversarial = f.get("Adversarial inputs", "(none specified)")
 114:     loc = f.get("LOC estimate", "(unspecified)")
 115:     user_blocked = f.get("User-blocked", "NO")
 116:     blocked_by = f.get("Blocked by", "(none)")
 117:     blocks = f.get("Blocks", "(none)")
 118: 
 119:     foundation_default_lines = [
 120:         "- `state/polaris_restart/plan.md` §4 (master breakdown)",
 121:         "- `polaris-controls/CHARTER.md` §1 + §3 + §4 + §7 (roles, LOC cap, immutable tests, visibility)",
 122:         "- `polaris-controls/PLAN.md` (slice progression context)",
 123:         f"- `docs/carney_delivery_plan_v6_2.md` Phase {phase} / Feature {feature}",
 124:     ]
 125:     if foundation:
 126:         foundation_default_lines.append(f"- {foundation}  (Issue-specific)")
 127:     foundation_block = "\n".join(foundation_default_lines)
 128: 
 129:     body = f"""## Phase / Feature
 130: 
 131: - **Phase:** {phase}
 132: - **Feature:** {feature}
 133: 
 134: ## Scope
 135: 
 136: {scope}
 137: 
 138: ## Foundation refs
 139: 
 140: {foundation_block}
 141: 
 142: ## Acceptance criteria
 143: 
 144: {acceptance}
 145: 
 146: ## Out of scope
 147: 
 148: {out_of_scope}
 149: 
 150: ## Adversarial inputs
 151: 
 152: {adversarial}
 153: 
 154: ## LOC estimate
 155: 
 156: {loc} (≤200 per CHARTER §3)
 157: 
 158: ## Per-Issue artifacts required at PR open (CHARTER §7)
 159: 
 160: - `.codex/{issue["id"]}/brief.md` (Claude-authored)
 161: - `.codex/{issue["id"]}/codex_brief_verdict.txt` (Codex APPROVE)
 162: - `.codex/{issue["id"]}/codex_diff.patch` (Claude-written diff with `# canonical-diff-sha256: <64-hex>` trailer)
 163: - `.codex/{issue["id"]}/codex_diff_audit.txt` (Codex APPROVE on Red-Team checklist)
 164: - `outputs/audits/{issue["id"]}/claude_audit.md` (Claude architect review)
 165: 
 166: ## Blocks
 167: 
 168: - **Blocked by:** {blocked_by}
 169: - **Blocks:** {blocks}
 170: - **User-blocked:** {user_blocked}
 171: 
 172: ---
 173: 
 174: _This Issue is one of 130 opened by PR-E from `state/polaris_restart/issue_breakdown.md` (Codex APPROVE iter 4). Branch convention: `bot/{issue["id"]}`. The codex-required.yml workflow (PR-D Codex APPROVE iter 7) gates merge on §3.0 5-artifact triple._
 175: """
 176:     return body
 177: 
 178: 
 179: def issue_label(issue: dict) -> list[str]:
 180:     """Return GitHub labels for the Issue based on phase + feature.
 181: 
 182:     Labels normalized to lowercase + hyphenated; rejects any label with
 183:     invalid GH characters (slash, asterisk, etc. — defense against bad
 184:     parses leaking into labels).
 185:     """
 186:     f = issue["fields"]
 187:     labels = []
 188: 
 189:     def safe_label(prefix: str, raw: str) -> str | None:
 190:         v = raw.strip().lower().replace(" ", "-")
 191:         # Strip non-alnum/hyphen chars to avoid GH label rejection
 192:         v = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9_-]+", "", v)
 193:         if not v:
 194:             return None
 195:         return f"{prefix}-{v}"
 196: 
 197:     phase = f.get("Phase", "").strip()
 198:     feature = f.get("Feature", "").strip()
 199:     if phase:
 200:         lbl = safe_label("phase", phase)
 201:         if lbl:
 202:             labels.append(lbl)
 203:     if feature:
 204:         lbl = safe_label("feature", feature)
 205:         if lbl:
 206:             labels.append(lbl)
 207:     if f.get("User-blocked", "NO").upper() == "YES":
 208:         labels.append("user-blocked")
 209:     return labels
 210: 
 211: 
 212: def gh_issue_create(issue: dict, body: str, labels: list[str]) -> int | None:
 213:     """Call `gh issue create` and return the new issue number, or None on error."""
 214:     title = f'{issue["id"]} — {issue["title_short"]}'
 215:     cmd = [
 216:         "gh", "issue", "create",
 217:         "--repo", GH_REPO,
 218:         "--title", title,
 219:         "--body", body,
 220:     ]
 221:     for label in labels:
 222:         cmd.extend(["--label", label])
 223:     try:
 224:         result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, check=True)
 225:         # `gh issue create` returns the URL; extract the number.
 226:         url = result.stdout.strip()
 227:         m = re.search(r"/issues/(\d+)$", url)
 228:         if m:
 229:             return int(m.group(1))
 230:         return None
 231:     except subprocess.CalledProcessError as exc:
 232:         print(f"ERROR: gh issue create failed for {issue['id']}: {exc.stderr}", file=sys.stderr)
 233:         return None
 234:

 277:         failed = 0
 278:         for issue in issues:
 279:             if issue["id"] in existing_map:

 281:                 skipped += 1

 287:             if number is None:
 288:                 failed += 1
 289:                 continue
 290:             existing_map[issue["id"]] = number
 291:             # Persist after each successful create so we can resume on failure

from pathlib import Path
import re
text=Path('state/polaris_restart/issue_breakdown.md').read_text(encoding='utf-8')
# Find field bullets with indented child bullets before next top-level field/header
field_blocks=[]
lines=text.splitlines()
for i,line in enumerate(lines):
    if re.match(r'"'^- '"\\*\\*["'^*]+:'"\\*\\*', line):
        child=[]
        j=i+1
        while j<len(lines) and not re.match(r'"'^(### |## |---|- '"\\*\\*["'^*]+:'"\\*\\*)', lines[j]):
            if re.match(r'"'^'"\\s+-\\s+', lines[j]): child.append((j+1,lines[j].strip()))
            j+=1
        if child:
            field_blocks.append((i+1,line.strip(),child[:5]))

for row in field_blocks[:30]:
    print(row)

from pathlib import Path
import re
text=Path('state/polaris_restart/issue_breakdown.md').read_text(encoding='utf-8')
field_blocks=[]
lines=text.splitlines()
for i,line in enumerate(lines):
    if re.match(r'"'^- '"\\*\\*["'^*]+:'"\\*\\*', line):
        child=[]
        j=i+1
        while j<len(lines) and not re.match(r'"'^(### |## |---|- '"\\*\\*["'^*]+:'"\\*\\*)', lines[j]):
            if re.match(r'"'^'"\\s+-\\s+', lines[j]): child.append((j+1,lines[j].strip()))
            j+=1
        if child:
            field_blocks.append((i+1,line.strip(),child))
print('top-level field bullets with child bullets:', len(field_blocks))
for parent_line,parent,children in field_blocks:
    print('parent', parent_line, parent)
    for lineno,child in children:
        print(' child', lineno, child)

    start=m.end(); end=len(src)
    nextm=re.search(r'"'^(?:#{2,3}'"\\s+(?:§\\d+\\s+)?)(I-[a-z0-9]{2,8}-[0-9]{3})\\s+[—-]\\s+', src[start:], re.M)

# Validate every rendered issue has exact section order and artifact names matching workflow vars.
dry=Path('state/polaris_restart/pr_e_issues_dryrun.txt').read_text(encoding='utf-8')
blocks=list(re.finditer(r'"'^## WOULD CREATE Issue (I-[a-z0-9]{2,8}-[0-9]{3})$(.*?)(?=''^---'"\\n\\n## WOULD CREATE Issue |\\Z)', dry, re.M|re.S))
section_names=['## Phase / Feature','## Scope','## Foundation refs','## Acceptance criteria','## Out of scope','## Adversarial inputs','## LOC estimate','## Per-Issue artifacts required at PR open (CHARTER §7)','## Blocks']
errors=[]
for m in blocks:
    iid=m.group(1); body=m.group(2)
    pos=[body.find(s) for s in section_names]
    if any(p<0 for p in pos) or pos "'!= sorted(pos):
        errors.append((iid,'"'section_order'))
    expected=[f'.codex/{iid}/brief.md',f'.codex/{iid}/codex_brief_verdict.txt',f'.codex/{iid}/codex_diff.patch',f'.codex/{iid}/codex_diff_audit.txt',f'outputs/audits/{iid}/claude_audit.md']
    got=[m.group(1) for m in re.finditer(r'"'^- `([''^`]+)`'"', body, re.M) if m.group(1).startswith('.codex/') or m.group(1).startswith('outputs/audits/')]
    if got "'!= expected:
        errors.append((iid,'"'artifacts',got))
print('rendered_blocks', len(blocks))
print('schema_artifact_errors', len(errors))
for e in errors[:10]: print(e)

 succeeded in 1545ms:
Create an issue on GitHub.

Adding an issue to projects requires authorization with the `project` scope.
To authorize, run `gh auth refresh -s project`.

The `--assignee` flag supports the following special values:
- `@me`: assign yourself
- `@copilot`: assign Copilot (not supported on GitHub Enterprise Server)


USAGE
  gh issue create [flags]

ALIASES
  gh issue new

FLAGS
  -a, --assignee login   Assign people by their login. Use "@me" to self-assign.
  -b, --body string      Supply a body. Will prompt for one otherwise.
  -F, --body-file file   Read body text from file (use "-" to read from standard input)
  -e, --editor           Skip prompts and open the text editor to write the title and body in. The first line is the title and the remaining text is the body.
  -l, --label name       Add labels by name
  -m, --milestone name   Add the issue to a milestone by name
  -p, --project title    Add the issue to projects by title
      --recover string   Recover input from a failed run of create
  -T, --template name    Template name to use as starting body text
  -t, --title string     Supply a title. Will prompt for one otherwise.
  -w, --web              Open the browser to create an issue

INHERITED FLAGS
      --help                     Show help for command
  -R, --repo [HOST/]OWNER/REPO   Select another repository using the [HOST/]OWNER/REPO format

EXAMPLES
  $ gh issue create --title "I found a bug" --body "Nothing works"
  $ gh issue create --label "bug,help wanted"
  $ gh issue create --label bug --label "help wanted"
  $ gh issue create --assignee monalisa,hubot
  $ gh issue create --assignee "@me"
  $ gh issue create --assignee "@copilot"
  $ gh issue create --project "Roadmap"
  $ gh issue create --template "Bug Report"

LEARN MORE
  Use `gh <command> <subcommand> --help` for more information about a command.
  Read the manual at https://cli.github.com/manual
  Learn about exit codes using `gh help exit-codes`
  Learn about accessibility experiences using `gh help accessibility`
